# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements

2 6 4 3 6 8 9
 ^gU1e6eyT

find the longest sub array with sum <= s
and then use the formula the number of subarrays
is left -right + 1.
pseudo code :

sum = 0 , left = 0 , right = 0 , ans = 0 
for right 0...n
    sum += a[right]
    while(sum > s)
        sum -= a[left++]
    if sum <= x
        ans += left -right +1

return ans; 
 ^tvg12u1r
